  MIN(?x_1, ?z) = MIN(?z, ?x_1)
  MIN(?z, ?b) = MIN(?b, ?z)
  MIN(?b_2, ?z) = MIN(?z, ?b_2)
  MIN(?z, ?b) = MIN(?b, ?z)
  MIN(?x, ?y) = MIN(?y, ?x)
  MIN(?y, ?b) = MIN(?b, ?y) }
